                        :ARG0 (s2 / sectarian)))
            :ARG1 (w / website
                  :mod (o / official)
                  :poss (p / person
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Ayatollah"
                              :op2 "Ali"
                              :op3 "al-Sistani")
                        :ARG0-of (l / lead-02
                              :ARG1 r2
                              :location (c2 / country
                                    :name (n3 / name
                                          :op1 "Iraq"))))))
      :op2 (b / block-01
            :ARG0 a2
            :ARG1 w))

                        :ARG1 (b / boundary)))

                                    :ARG0 g
                                    :ARG1 (c5 / crime-02
                                          :ARG1 (v / various)))))))
      :time (r / recent))
